ll N = sizeof(w)/sizeof(w[0]);
ll k = 8, h = 9, l = 19;

double dist(double a[], double b[])
{
    double d = 0;
    ll i = 0;
    for (i = 0; i < 24; i++)
        d += abs(a[i] - b[i]);

    return d;
}

void gettemps(double x[], double p[], bool bSkip = false)
{
    ll j;
    double dd, dd2, r = dist(x, w[0]);
    multiset <pair<double, ll>> s;
    s.insert({r, 0});
    for (j = 1; j < N; j++)
        if ((r = dist(x, w[j])) < s.rbegin()->first)
        {
            if (r == 0 && bSkip) continue;
            s.insert({r, j});
            if (s.size() > l)
            {
                auto it = s.end();
                s.erase(--it);
            }

        }
    double avg[36] = {0};
    for (auto [r, j]:s)
    {
        for(ll ii = 23; ii < 36; ii++)
        avg[ii] += w[j][ii];
    }
    for (ll ii = 23; ii < 36; ii++)
        avg[ii] /= l;

    dd = x[23] - avg[23];
    dd2 = 2*x[23] - x[22] - x[0];
    for (j = 0; j < 12; j++)
    {
        double y = dd + avg[j+24], z = dd2+x[j];
        p[j] = (y*h + z)/(h+1);
    }
}

int main()
{
    ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(0);
    ll i, n;
    k = 7, l = 26, h = 12;
    double x[24], p[12];
    cin >> n;
    while(n--)
    {
        for (i = 0; i < 24; i++)
            cin >> x[i];

        gettemps(x, p);
        for (i = 0; i < k; i++)
        {
            cout << setprecision(1) << fixed << p[i] << " ";
        }

        for (; i < 12; i++)
            cout << "? ";
        cout << "\n";
    }
    return 0;
}
